The coordinator manages consumer group membership, partition assignment, offset commits, and timeout handling. While the test suite is comprehensive (~25,900 lines), there are specific failure modes and edge cases that warrant additional regression tests to improve resilience and maintainability.\n\nThe identified gaps focus on:\n1. **Concurrent operation race conditions** - Member joins/leaves during assignment transitions\n2. **Timeout expiration edge cases** - Timeout races with member state changes\n3. **Assignment validation failures** - Partition assignor exceptions during specific states\n4. **Metadata update synchronization** - State transitions during topology changes\n5. **Resource cleanup violations** - Precondition failures in tombstone replay\n6. **Transactional offset failure paths** - Error handling in txn-based offset commits\n7. **Member epoch validation edge cases** - Fencing conditions with concurrent heartbeats\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Concurrent Member Join During Unrevoked Partition State\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4809-4900 (consumerGroupHeartbeat method), ~lines 1562-1595 (throwIfConsumerGroupMemberEpochIsInvalid)\n\n**Description**: When a member is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state (waiting to acknowledge partition revocation), a concurrent heartbeat from a different member joining the group can trigger a new assignment computation. The test should verify that the joining member's epoch correctly reflects the assignment update, and the existing member in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state is not incorrectly fenced or has its timeout cancelled.\n\n**Root Cause**: The member epoch validation uses point-in-time checks without verifying that concurrent operations don't create epoch invariant violations. If one member's heartbeat triggers group epoch bump while another is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, edge case handling is unclear.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConcurrentMemberJoinDuringUnrevokedPartitionsState() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = setupContextWithTopic(topicId, \"test-topic\", 4);\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = createAssignor(context);\n\n    // Member 1 joins, gets assigned partitions 0,1,2\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId1, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    int epoch1 = result1.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(1, epoch1, \"First member should receive epoch 1\");\n\n    // Prepare new assignment with member 2\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1))),\n        memberId2, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 2, 3))))));\n\n    // Member 2 joins while member 1 is still in stable state\n    // This should trigger new group epoch\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result2 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId2, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    int epoch2 = result2.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(2, epoch2, \"Second member should receive epoch 2\");\n\n    // Member 1 now receives new assignment (epoch 1) and transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\n    // because it's losing partition 2\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1_revoke =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId1, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(1, result1_revoke.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member 1 should still be at epoch 1, waiting to revoke\");\n    assertTrue(hasAssignedPartitions(result1_revoke.response(), topicId, List.of(0, 1)),\n        \"Member 1 should be assigned partitions 0,1\");\n\n    // While member 1 is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state, member 3 joins\n    String memberId3 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0))),\n        memberId2, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 1, 2))),\n        memberId3, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 3))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result3 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId3, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(3, result3.response().memberEpoch(), \"Third member should receive epoch 3\");\n\n    // Member 1 should NOT be fenced yet; it should receive bump to epoch 3 in next heartbeat\n    // but should still be in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1_ack =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId1, 1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(3, result1_ack.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member 1 should be bumped to epoch 3\");\n    assertTrue(hasAssignedPartitions(result1_ack.response(), topicId, List.of(0)),\n        \"Member 1 should be assigned partition 0\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Exercises `consumerGroupHeartbeat()` call sequence with 3+ concurrent members\n- Validates epoch state machine transitions during concurrent joins (lines 4809-4900)\n- Tests member epoch validation during UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state (lines 1562-1595)\n- Covers group epoch bump with concurrent pending assignments\n- Validates no spurious member fencing or timeout cancellation\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Rebalance Timeout Expiration Race with Member Epoch Update\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4641-4673 (scheduleConsumerGroupRebalanceTimeout), ~lines 1562-1595 (member epoch validation)\n\n**Description**: A rebalance timeout is scheduled when a member transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state. If the member updates its epoch (by acknowledging revocation) just before the timeout fires, the timeout handler must check the epoch to avoid fencing the member incorrectly. The test should verify that a timeout fired after epoch update is a no-op. Additionally, if the timeout fires while a new heartbeat with epoch update is in-flight, the coordinator must correctly handle the race.\n\n**Root Cause**: The timeout handler checks `if (member.memberEpoch() == memberEpoch)` to determine if timeout is stale, but concurrent heartbeat processing can create a narrow window where both the timeout and new heartbeat try to update state.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testRebalanceTimeoutExpirationRaceWithMemberEpochUpdate() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    long rebalanceTimeoutMs = 5000;\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = setupContextWithTopic(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3);\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = createAssignor(context);\n\n    // Member joins and gets assignment\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId, 0,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), rebalanceTimeoutMs));\n    int epoch1 = joinResult.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(1, epoch1);\n\n    // Prepare new assignment that removes partitions for this member\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0))))));\n\n    // Trigger rebalance by calling heartbeat\n    // This schedules rebalance timeout as member transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> revokeResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), rebalanceTimeoutMs));\n    assertEquals(1, revokeResult.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should still be at epoch 1 in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\");\n\n    // Capture scheduled timeout\n    ScheduledTimeout<CoordinatorRecord> timeout =\n        context.assertRebalanceTimeout(groupId, memberId, (int) rebalanceTimeoutMs);\n\n    // Advance time just before timeout fires\n    List<CoordinatorRecord> records = context.sleep(rebalanceTimeoutMs - 100);\n    assertEquals(0, records.size(), \"No timeout should fire yet\");\n\n    // Member sends heartbeat with revocation ack before timeout fires\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> ackResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), // Member acknowledges by sending topicPartitions\n            new TopicPartitions(topicId, List.of(0))));\n    int epoch2 = ackResult.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertTrue(epoch2 > epoch1, \"Member should advance to next epoch\");\n\n    // Now advance time enough for original timeout to fire\n    records = context.sleep(200);\n    // Timeout should fire but find that member epoch has changed, so it's a no-op\n    assertEquals(0, records.size(),\n        \"Timeout should be no-op since member epoch has advanced\");\n\n    // Member should still be in group and not fenced\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeat =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch2,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertNotNull(heartbeat.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should still be in group and not fenced\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `scheduleConsumerGroupRebalanceTimeout()` with concurrent member state changes (lines 4641-4673)\n- Validates timeout epoch check correctly identifies stale timeouts\n- Exercises race condition between timeout firing and member epoch update\n- Covers no-op case when timeout finds epoch mismatch\n- Tests member state machine continuity through timeout race\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Partition Assignor Exception During Member Replacement\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4309-4415 (replaceMember), ~lines 2900-3000 (target assignment computation), ~lines 3874-3878 (PartitionAssignorException handling)\n\n**Description**: When a new static member with the same instance ID replaces an existing member, the coordinator must compute a new target assignment. If the partition assignor throws `PartitionAssignorException` during this computation, the request should fail with `UnknownServerException`, but the existing member should remain in the group (not removed). The test verifies that member replacement is atomic with respect to assignor failures.\n\n**Root Cause**: Member replacement includes both removal of old member and addition of new member. If assignor fails after old member removal but before response is sent, the group could be left in inconsistent state.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testPartitionAssignorExceptionDuringStaticMemberReplacement() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String instanceId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = setupContextWithTopic(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3);\n\n    // Use a mock assignor that will fail on second assignment\n    ConsumerGroupPartitionAssignor assignor = mock(ConsumerGroupPartitionAssignor.class);\n    when(assignor.name()).thenReturn(\"range\");\n\n    // First assignment succeeds\n    when(assignor.assign(any(), any()))\n        .thenReturn(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n            memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n                mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))))\n        .thenThrow(new PartitionAssignorException(\"Assignment failed on replacement\"));\n\n    context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .withMetadataImage(setupMetadataImage(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3))\n        .build();\n\n    // First member joins successfully\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId1)\n                .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                .setGroupInstanceId(instanceId)\n                .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n\n    assertEquals(1, joinResult.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"First member should receive epoch 1\");\n    assertEquals(memberId1, joinResult.response().memberId());\n\n    // Verify group state has member 1\n    ConsumerGroup group = (ConsumerGroup) context.getGroupOrThrow(groupId);\n    assertTrue(group.hasMember(memberId1), \"Group should have member 1\");\n    assertEquals(1, group.numMembers(), \"Group should have 1 member\");\n\n    // Different member (memberId2) tries to join with same instance ID\n    // This should trigger assignor, which will fail\n    UnknownServerException thrown = assertThrows(UnknownServerException.class, () ->\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId2)\n                .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                .setGroupInstanceId(instanceId)\n                .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\"))));\n\n    assertTrue(thrown.getMessage().contains(\"Assignment failed\"),\n        \"Exception should contain assignor error\");\n\n    // Verify that original member is STILL in group despite assignor failure\n    group = (ConsumerGroup) context.getGroupOrThrow(groupId);\n    assertTrue(group.hasMember(memberId1),\n        \"Original member should still be in group after assignor failure\");\n    assertEquals(1, group.numMembers(),\n        \"Group should still have 1 member, not replaced\");\n\n    // Original member should still be able to heartbeat\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeat =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId1, 1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertNotNull(heartbeat.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Original member should still be in group\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `replaceMember()` method with assignor exception (lines 4309-4415)\n- Validates exception handling in target assignment computation (lines 2900-3000, 3874-3878)\n- Covers atomicity of member replacement operation\n- Verifies group state consistency after assignor failure\n- Tests static member instance ID recovery after failed replacement\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Concurrent Heartbeat and Timeout Expiration with Member Fencing\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4460-4473 (scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout), ~lines 4426-4440 (cancelGroupSessionTimeout), ~lines 1562-1595 (member epoch validation)\n\n**Description**: A session timeout is scheduled when a member joins a consumer group. If the member heartbeats with a stale epoch while the session timeout fires, both operations try to update the member state. The test verifies that the timeout correctly checks if the member is still at the expected state before fencing, preventing double-fencing or fencing healthy members.\n\n**Root Cause**: Session timeout handler doesn't verify all preconditions before modifying member state. Concurrent heartbeat processing can race with timeout, causing inconsistent state transitions.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testSessionTimeoutRaceWithConcurrentHeartbeat() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    int sessionTimeoutMs = 3000;\n    int heartbeatIntervalMs = 1000;\n\n The coordinator manages consumer group membership, partition assignment, offset commits, and timeout handling. While the test suite is comprehensive (~25,900 lines), there are specific failure modes and edge cases that warrant additional regression tests to improve resilience and maintainability.\n\nThe identified gaps focus on:\n1. **Concurrent operation race conditions** - Member joins/leaves during assignment transitions\n2. **Timeout expiration edge cases** - Timeout races with member state changes\n3. **Assignment validation failures** - Partition assignor exceptions during specific states\n4. **Metadata update synchronization** - State transitions during topology changes\n5. **Resource cleanup violations** - Precondition failures in tombstone replay\n6. **Transactional offset failure paths** - Error handling in txn-based offset commits\n7. **Member epoch validation edge cases** - Fencing conditions with concurrent heartbeats\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Concurrent Member Join During Unrevoked Partition State\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4809-4900 (consumerGroupHeartbeat method), ~lines 1562-1595 (throwIfConsumerGroupMemberEpochIsInvalid)\n\n**Description**: When a member is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state (waiting to acknowledge partition revocation), a concurrent heartbeat from a different member joining the group can trigger a new assignment computation. The test should verify that the joining member's epoch correctly reflects the assignment update, and the existing member in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state is not incorrectly fenced or has its timeout cancelled.\n\n**Root Cause**: The member epoch validation uses point-in-time checks without verifying that concurrent operations don't create epoch invariant violations. If one member's heartbeat triggers group epoch bump while another is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, edge case handling is unclear.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testConcurrentMemberJoinDuringUnrevokedPartitionsState() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = assignor = createAssignor(context);\n\n    // Member 1 joins, gets assigned partitions 0,1,2\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId1, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    int epoch1 = result1.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(1, epoch1, \"First member should receive epoch 1\");\n\n    // Prepare new assignment with member 2\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1))),\n        memberId2, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 2, 3))))));\n\n    // Member 2 joins while member 1 is still in stable state\n    // This should trigger new group epoch\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result2 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId2, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    int epoch2 = result2.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(2, epoch2, \"Second member should receive epoch 2\");\n\n    // Member 1 now receives new assignment (epoch 1) and transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\n    // because it's losing partition 2\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1_revoke =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId1, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(1, result1_revoke.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member 1 should still be at epoch 1, waiting to revoke\");\n    assertTrue(hasAssignedPartitions(result1_revoke.response(), topicId, List.of(0, 1)),\n        \"Member 1 should be assigned partitions 0,1\");\n\n    // While member 1 is in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state, member 3 joins\n    String memberId3 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0))),\n        memberId2, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 1, 2))),\n        memberId3, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 3))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result3 =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId3, 0, List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(3, result3.response().memberEpoch(), \"Third member should receive epoch 3\");\n\n    // Member 1 should NOT be fenced yet; it should receive bump to epoch 3 in next heartbeat\n    // but should still be in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> result1_ack =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId1, 1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertEquals(3, result1_ack.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member 1 should be bumped to epoch 3\");\n    assertTrue(hasAssignedPartitions(result1_ack.response(), topicId, List.of(0)),\n        \"Member 1 should be assigned partition 0\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Exercises `consumerGroupHeartbeat()` call sequence with 3+ concurrent members\n- HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4641-4673 (scheduleConsumerGroupRebalanceTimeout), ~lines 1562-1595 (member epoch validation)\n\n**Description**: A rebalance timeout is scheduled when a member transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state. If the member updates its epoch (by acknowledging revocation) just before the timeout fires, the timeout handler must check the epoch to avoid fencing the member incorrectly. The test should verify that a timeout fired after epoch update is a no-op. Additionally, if the timeout fires while a new heartbeat with epoch update is in-flight, the coordinator must correctly handle the race.\n\n**Root Cause**: The timeout handler checks `if (member.memberEpoch() == memberEpoch)` to determine if timeout is stale, but concurrent heartbeat processing can create a narrow window where both the timeout and new heartbeat try to update state.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testRebalanceTimeoutExpirationRaceWithMemberEpochUpdate() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String memberId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n    long rebalanceTimeoutMs = 5000;\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = setupContextWithTopic(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3);\n    MockPartitionAssignor assignor = createAssignor(context);\n\n    // Member joins and gets assignment\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n            mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))));\n\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(joinRequest(groupId, memberId, 0,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), rebalanceTimeoutMs));\n    int epoch1 = joinResult.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(1, epoch1);\n\n    // Prepare new assignment that removes partitions for this member\n    assignor.prepareGroupAssignment(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n        memberId, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0))))));\n\n    // Trigger rebalance by calling heartbeat\n    // This schedules rebalance timeout as member transitions to UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> revokeResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), rebalanceTimeoutMs));\n    assertEquals(1, revokeResult.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should still be at epoch 1 in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS\");\n\n    // Capture scheduled timeout\n    ScheduledTimeout<CoordinatorRecord> timeout =\n        context.assertRebalanceTimeout(groupId, memberId, (int) rebalanceTimeoutMs);\n\n    // Advance time just before timeout fires\n    List<CoordinatorRecord> records = context.sleep(rebalanceTimeoutMs - 100);\n    assertEquals(0, records.size(), \"No timeout should fire yet\");\n\n    // Member sends heartbeat with revocation ack before timeout fires\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> ackResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch1,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\"), // Member acknowledges by sending topicPartitions\n            new TopicPartitions(topicId, List.of(0))));\n    int epoch2 = ackResult.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertTrue(epoch2 > epoch1, \"Member should advance to next epoch\");\n\n    // Now advance time enough for original timeout to fire\n    records = context.sleep(200);\n    // Timeout should fire but find that member epoch has changed, so it's a no-op\n    assertEquals(0, records.size(),\n        \"Timeout should be no-op since member epoch has advanced\");\n\n    // Member should still be in group and not fenced\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeat =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(heartbeatRequest(groupId, memberId, epoch2,\n            List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n    assertNotNull(heartbeat.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should still be in group and not fenced\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- Tests `scheduleConsumerGroupRebalanceTimeout()` with concurrent member state changes (lines 4641-4673)\n- Validates timeout epoch check correctly identifies stale timeouts\n- Exercises race condition between timeout firing and member epoch update\n- Covers no-op case when timeout finds epoch mismatch\n- Tests member state machine continuity through timeout race\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Partition Assignor Exception During Member Replacement\n\n**Risk**: MEDIUM\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4309-4415 (replaceMember), ~lines 2900-3000 (target assignment computation), ~lines 3874-3878 (PartitionAssignorException handling)\n\n**Description**: When a new static member with the same instance ID replaces an existing member, the coordinator must compute a new target assignment. If the partition assignor throws `PartitionAssignorException` during this computation, the request should fail with `UnknownServerException`, but the existing member should remain in the group (not removed). The test verifies that member replacement is atomic with respect to assignor failures.\n\n**Root Cause**: Member replacement includes both removal of old member and addition of new member. If assignor fails after old member removal but before response is sent, the group could be left in inconsistent state.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testPartitionAssignorExceptionDuringStaticMemberReplacement() {\n    String groupId = \"testGroup\";\n    String instanceId = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId1 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    String memberId2 = Uuid.randomUuid().toString();\n    Uuid topicId = Uuid.randomUuid();\n\n    GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = setupContextWithTopic(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3);\n\n    // Use a mock assignor that will fail on second assignment\n    ConsumerGroupPartitionAssignor assignor = mock(ConsumerGroupPartitionAssignor.class);\n    when(assignor.name()).thenReturn(\"range\");\n\n    // First assignment succeeds\n    when(assignor.assign(any(), any()))\n        .thenReturn(new GroupAssignment(Map.of(\n            memberId1, new MemberAssignmentImpl(mkAssignment(\n                mkTopicAssignment(topicId, 0, 1, 2))))))\n        .thenThrow(new PartitionAssignorException(\"Assignment failed on replacement\"));\n\n    context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n        .withConfig(GroupCoordinatorConfig.CONSUMER_GROUP_ASSIGNORS_CONFIG, List.of(assignor))\n        .withMetadataImage(setupMetadataImage(topicId, \"test-topic\", 3))\n        .build();\n\n    // First member joins successfully\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> joinResult =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId1)\n                .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                .setGroupInstanceId(instanceId)\n                .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n\n    assertEquals(1, joinResult.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"First member should receive epoch 1\");\n    assertEquals(memberId1, joinResult.response().memberId());\n\n    // Verify group state has member 1\n    ConsumerGroup group = (ConsumerGroup) context.getGroupOrThrow(groupId);\n    assertTrue(group.hasMember(memberId1), \"Group should have member 1\");\n    assertEquals(1, group.numMembers(), \"Group with Member Fencing\n\n**Risk**: HIGH\n\n**Code Location**: GroupMetadataManager.java ~lines 4460-4473 (scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout), ~lines 4426-4440 (cancelGroupSessionTimeout), ~lines 1562-1595 (member epoch validation)\n\n**Description**: A session timeout is scheduled when a member joins a consumer group. If the member heartbeats with a stale epoch while the session timeout fires, both operations try to update the member state. The test verifies that the timeout correctly checks if the member is still at the expected state before fencing, preventing double-fencing or fencing healthy members.\n\n**Root Cause**: Session timeout handler doesn't verify all preconditions before modifying member state. Concurrent heartbeat processing can race with timeout, causing inconsistent state transitions.\n\n**Proposed Test**:\n```java\n@Test\npublic void testSessionTimeoutRaceWithConcurrentHeartbeat() {\n .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId)\n                .setMemberEpoch(0)\n                .setRebalanceTimeoutMs(5000)\n                .setSessionTimeoutMs(sessionTimeoutMs)\n                .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n\n    int epoch1 = joinResult.response().memberEpoch();\n    assertEquals(1, epoch1);\n    assertEquals(heartbeatIntervalMs, joinResult.response().heartbeatIntervalMs());\n\n    // Session timeout is scheduled\n    ScheduledTimeout<CoordinatorRecord> sessionTimeout =\n        context.assertSessionTimeout(groupId, memberId);\n    assertNotNull(sessionTimeout, \"Session timeout should be scheduled\");\n\n    // Advance time to just before session timeout\n    context.sleep(sessionTimeoutMs - 100);\n\n    // Member sends heartbeat just as session timeout is about to fire\n    CoordinatorResult<ConsumerGroupHeartbeatResponseData, CoordinatorRecord> heartbeat =\n        context.consumerGroupHeartbeat(\n            new ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData()\n                .setGroupId(groupId)\n                .setMemberId(memberId)\n                .setMemberEpoch(epoch1)\n                .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n\n    assertEquals(epoch1, heartbeat.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should remain at same epoch for regular heartbeat\");\n\n    // .setSubscribedTopicNames(List.of(\"test-topic\")));\n\n    assertNotNull(followupHeartbeat.response().memberEpoch(),\n        \"Member should remain in group\");\n}\n```\n\n**Coverage Delta**:\n- The test should verify that the joining member's epoch correctly reflects the assignment update, and the existing member in UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS state is not incorrectly fenced or has its timeout cancelled.\n\n**Root Cause**: The member epoch validation uses point-in-time checks without verifying that concurrent operations don't create epoch invariant violations.
